Content-Type: text/plain; charset="UTF-8"

Hi

I am TIMLEGGE on PAUSE.

Net::SAML2 seems to be dormant and there has not been a release since
2012 despite there being a number of issues in issues log and an open
issue on github.

I have contacted Neil Bowers NEILB and Chris Andrews CHRISA (former
Primary maintainer) to no avail.

While Neil has expressed an intention to update a github repo and get
things patched my first contact to him was almost a year ago.  See
attached (sorry for the pdfs).

I realize the Neil has a substantial number of modules on his list and
Net::SAML2 is just one more.

I have a github repo at https://github.com/timlegge/perl-Net-SAML2
which currently appears to be the most up to date version and it is a
version that I use daily in a Foswiki installation in combination with
https://foswiki.org/Extensions/SamlLoginContrib which I wrote.

I have also packaged the module based on my git repo in an Alpine
package that I have included in timlegge/docker-foswiki that is now
being used by a few people.  Once an updated version of the module is
released I plan to officially submit it to the aports project of
AlpineLinux as part of the community repo.

I have a vested interest in ensuring that a module gets released and
updated and gets bugs addressed.

Chris released a useful piece of code and to my knowledge it is the
best available SAML2 module for Perl. It would be unfortunate for that
effort to have been wasted.

I am fine with Neil continuing to be a co maintainer but I would like
to volunteer to be the primary maintainer.

Please let me know if you need more information or if you need me to
try additional communication.  I realize that this is a bad time to be
asking unfortunately I would like to see this module finally
up-to-date.

regards

Timothy Legge
Moncton, NB CANADA

--0000000000001ae9e505a23960ab
